<Z>Gridiron Stats <C> Has just restarted for the new season, with a couple of pre-season turns to roster shuffle prior to the<L.31.1>
start of the new season. Ask if you want details, or see www.pbmsports.com or send a fiver for a startup and first three turns.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>PDF Reports <C> Emailed game reports in Gameplan Baseball and Gridstats are now available as PDF files. All other games will<L.31.1>
follow as soon as I'm able to get the software programmed (so please be patient - it'll take me a few weeks to program every game.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
I won't change your game reports from "Text" to "PDF" until you ask me to, and if you want a trial of a PDF report let me know.<L.31.1>
You should find PDF reports rather easier to cope with - Adobe Reader is free to download (see www.pbmsports.com for a link) and<L.31.1>
you can open your reports with one click of the mouse (indeed, you don't need a printer, though most will then print from it) and<L.31.1>
you don't need to worry about dodgy email clients messing up the formatting, or printer drivers. If you want to stay with the text<L.31.1>
format that's fine but I only expect people will want to do so if you can't make Adobe Reader work (which is pretty unlikely) or<L.31.1>
if you use the text file for other purposes (such as exporting the stats into some software you've produced yourself).<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
If you've not tried email reports before, or you've had problems, try out the PDF. It really is very straightforward.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Hotmail Users <C> A side effect of the above change (and the new bit of kit we use that sends out reports as Text or PDF)<L.31.1>
apparently means that game reports sent to Hotmail no longer arrive as attachments (not that they were ever meant to, the whole<L.31.1>
reason all of this stuff can be so tricky is email clients basically doing their own thing, and reformatting them for you<L.31.1>
according to "what they think you want" - hence the change to PDF files). AOL is often worse for doing this than Hotmail!<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
Anyway, the answer for Hotmail users is that instead of saving the attachment (as you used to) you need to File and Save the<L.31.1>
message as a text file (which is what most other systems already do) and then you should be able to print from that.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
And meanwhile, hopefully it won't be too long before the PDF option is available in all games here (Gameplan Baseball and Gridiron<L.31.1>
Stats only at the moment) and all of this hassle and nonsense will be something of the past.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Credit Card Payments <C> If you want to pay by credit card over the Internet you now have the option of paying in Sterling, US<L.31.1>
Dollars or Aussie Dollars, whichever you prefer. Cheques are still fine as well, and actually mean slightly lower charges for us!<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Websites <C> The website for submitting orders is at www.softsim.co.uk. www.pbmsports.com is our main "static" information<L.31.1>
website, as well as news of what's going on here. For news of what is happening with Pete in Yeovil see www.sidetracks.co.uk. For<L.31.1>
information on baseball and how it works, see www.howbaseballworks.com - a site also designed for recruiting new punters!<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Internet Orders <C> Should be submitted online by 9am. The confirmation that they've been received by us is the page that comes<L.31.1>
up in response to you pushing the button. When you see that page, your orders are in. The version that's emailed to you is just<L.31.1>
for information - we email it to save you having to copy and paste or save it as a screenshot. If the email copy of your orders<L.31.1>
doesn't appear don't worry - emails get delayed or go missing quite often (far more than some people think). The more people who<L.1.1>
<P>
<L>
<L.1.1>
submit orders via the internet the better - if you want more information, just ask. You can also pay for credits online.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Email Results <C> Emailed results are normally sent out between 3pm and 6pm. If there's a delay in processing, it'll say so on<L.31.1>
www.pbmsports.com - please check there first. If you haven't received emailed results 24 hours after they're due, then email me<L.31.1>
and ask for them to be resent. Don't ask me before the 24 hours are due, but don't wait much longer either. <L.31.1>
